## üéØ About

> *"The key to artificial intelligence has always been the representation."* ‚Äî Jeff Hawkins

This repository is a **living collection** of research papers exploring the exciting intersection of **Neuro-Symbolic AI** and **Large Language Models**. We track cutting-edge research on how symbolic reasoning can enhance LLMs, and vice versa.

### ‚ú® Features

| | Feature | Description |
|:--:|:--------|:------------|
| üîÑ | **Auto-Updated** | New papers fetched daily from ArXiv |
| ‚≠ê | **Top-Tier Highlighted** | Papers from A* venues (NeurIPS, ICML, ACL, EMNLP...) |
| üè∑Ô∏è | **Well-Organized** | Categorized by research topics |
| üîó | **Code Included** | Links to official implementations |

---

## ü§î Why Neuro-Symbolic + LLM?

### üß™ The Problem

LLMs are powerful but struggle with:
- ‚ùå Complex multi-step logical reasoning
- ‚ùå Mathematical proofs and formal verification  
- ‚ùå Consistent rule following
- ‚ùå Explainable, verifiable decisions

### üí° The Solution

Neuro-Symbolic approaches provide:
- ‚úÖ Formal logical reasoning with theorem provers
- ‚úÖ SAT/SMT solvers for constraint satisfaction
- ‚úÖ Verifiable and provably correct computation
- ‚úÖ Interpretable step-by-step reasoning chains

### üîó The Fusion

Combining LLMs with symbolic AI enables:

```
Natural Language ‚Üí LLM Parser ‚Üí Formal Logic ‚Üí Symbolic Solver ‚Üí Verified Result ‚Üí Natural Language
```

- üßÆ Solve complex math with provable correctness
- üéØ Achieve faithful logical reasoning
- üîç Provide explainable AI decisions

---

## üìö Research Topics

| Topic | Description | Key Papers |
|:------|:------------|:-----------|
| üîó **LLM + Solvers** | LLMs with theorem provers, SAT/SMT solvers | Logic-LM, LINC, SatLM |
| ‚õìÔ∏è **Symbolic CoT** | Chain-of-thought with formal logic | SymbCoT, Faithful CoT |
| üß† **Neuro-Symbolic** | Hybrid neural-symbolic architectures | NeurASP, DeepProbLog |
| üìê **Math Reasoning** | Theorem proving & math problem solving | AlphaProof, LEGO-Prover |
| üéì **Curated Classics** | Hand-picked influential papers | See below |
